< review>
As a Marine Corps family, we have been away from our home town for over 25 years.
As a mother, my job is to find the best of the best when it comes to the providers that I entrust to examine my children.
With all the positive reviews, I thought I had done just that!
The staff was ABSOLUTELY AMAZING!  They were very kind and receptive.
We waited for Dr. Schneider for over 25 minutes past our appointment time.  Why?  Because he was busy going out of his way for an older "upper class" woman who was being overly repetitive about her concerns towards contact lenses.
Dr. Schneider finally walks in our room.  He, unlike his staff, came off as rude and dismissive when I was trying to explain my daughter's medical history with him.  Afterall, this was our new patient visit.  During my explanation, he kept interrupting me by asking how my daughter's unexplained seizures were of any relevance to him.  I was furious to say the least!
I expected the same courtesy that he had given to the woman before us.  He did not extend the same politeness or patience that he had with his previous
client.  He actually rushed through our whole exam!  Why?  Because the lady prior to us made him late for all his other clients.  We may not look wealthy, but I can assure you, we are a wealthy and highly educated family.  We do not go out of our way to flaunt it like most people In order to recieve "special" treatment.
I will NEVER visit your store again!
Oh, and that $39 out of pocket exam you offer with your fancy machine, is not so special AT ALL!  Our Texas optometrist, DR. 3 stars only because the guy who helped me was very nice. As a used car buyer, learn to ask questions and always have a mechanic look over the car you‚Äôre interested in.

After test driving the car - first thing the manager said to me was ‚Äúso how do you want to pay?‚Äù I said hold on hold on. I asked for the Carfax report - turns out the car had been in an accident. Which can be ok, but after I had a mechanic come to look at the repair job .. turns out the car was a disaster. It was not welded correctly, the battery moved all around out of place, other pieces were unstable/missing screws, and there was rust in the car.

Not to mention the price was a bit fishy. If it was in good shape, it would have been fine. But the car was truly a disaster, and they also claimed the DMV title transfer was ‚Äú$400‚Äù which in no way is true.

*When buying a used car here are the steps you need to take:

Inspect car for scrapes and dents on the outside

Inspect inside for rips and cleanliness/smell

Test drive car - first without AC or radio so you can hear if there are any unusual sounds

Ask for a Carfax report. See if the car has been in any accidents, and how many owners the car has had

Ask for the WALK AWAY price of the car. They always hit you with high tax and fees

Negotiate

Have a mechanic take a look

If all checks out, and you‚Äôre happy with the walk away price, Buy the car.<//Text>

< text>
Let me preface my comments by saying that the staff is wonderful and courteous at all times. Jeremy the General Manager has always been cordial and professional.

My review is in reference to the recent changes that have been made to this location, specifically the XGT class. I pay my monthly dues, and I find it very inconvenient that members are now limited as to when the aerobics room is available.  I being one of MANY members who are getting increasingly irritated with not being able to utilize the gym facilities as stated in the terms and conditions in our contract. Where does it say that by paying my monthly dues,  it therefore permits my use of the aerobics room on all days EXCEPT Tue, Thur, and Sat due to this ‚Äúclass‚Äù? In an effort to cash in on another revenue stream, Body exchange has decided to implement a ‚Äúgym‚Äù within a gym.  A class comprised of a total of 5-6 people at any given time forcing the other members to work around this waste of a class.

First they decided to demolish the ladies spa gym (which I paid EXTRA) in order for my wife and daughters to utilize. Then they justify that extra  cost by telling me it‚Äôs to provide me with towel service. Now with this new inconvenience of a class, I can no longer enjoy the gym as desired. At this point after many years of being a Body Exchange member, I can whole heartedly say that it‚Äôs time for a change. I‚Äôd rather pay extra and drive further to your competitor, than half to deal with this gym‚Äôs shortcomings.  I will no longer support this gym‚Äôs continuous goal to nickel and dime.< /text>

< Text>
Way to stingy! I was mortified to see that I ordered a shrimp cocktail and had absolutely no shrimp. I put my spoon into this monstrous cup of pure water. I poured all the water into another bowl to see how many shrimp if any were in there. After the cocktail cost me 12$ they gave me a full cup of cocktail juice with hardly any veggies and 10 medium shrimp. Not even large shrimp. I talked to a friend she said they did the same to her with the albondigas ( meatball) literally just 1 meatball. That is ridiculous! The only reason I gave it 2 stars was because at least they gave me back my 12$ and I gave them their cup of juice back. It was just an inconvenience. Maybe the boss needs to go eat at Ceviche loco, or Tacazo, or El pescador so that he can see what a shrimp cocktail actually looks like. I should have known they specialize on burgers not coctails. But if your going to offer this as part of your menu do it right. NEVER AGAIN! :(< /Text>

<date>1571688572494</date><Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
I was referred to Fix Auto following a car crash by my AAA Insurance. Fix Auto made the entire process very easy.

They accomodated my schedule, gave an accurate initial estimate of the total cost, called me a Lyft to Hertz, and took care of things between themselves and my insurance such that I did not have to do anything except leave and pick up the car.

There is one final important thing that I wanted to highlight. The day after I took my car back from Fix Auto, I had to take my car to my dealership because there was something wrong with the brake lights. This turned out to be an issue with a recalled part, not related to Fix Auto. During the visit, I had a Subaru (my manufacturer) technician do a full diagnostic on the engine (just for my peace of mind). He reported back that everything was in working order but more importantly, the technician was pleasantly surprised that every single thing was put back together the correct way. He told me that in his experience, when he services cars that have come from an external auto repair shop, minor things are not in put back in the right place.

I had a great experience with Fix Auto. Would definitely recommend.< /review>

< Review>
I love history and this is part of ours in the USA. We were visiting family in Sacramento and took a stroll through Old Town. This is where the Pony Express ended and it started in St. Joseph (Joe) Missouri. It only lasted 18 months (April 3 1860-October 26 1861) due to the Trans-Atlantic Telegraph being completed. But in it‚Äôs heyday it they could travel on horseback 1800 miles in 10 days. Quite a feat in those days.< /Review>
